[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 2 - RESOLVE CONVERSATIONAL CONTEXT:[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- If question contains "that", "it", "this value" â†’ use the most recent result from conversation history[0m                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Example: Previous answer was 78.93, question asks "what is that divided by 100?" â†’ use 78.93[0m                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the previous year" â†’ identify specific year from context[0m                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 3 - DATA EXTRACTION:[0m                                                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- For ambiguous cases, choose the value that makes business sense for the question[0m                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Preserve negative signs for declines, losses, decreases[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are signs correct (positive/negative)?[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 1 - UNDERSTAND THE QUESTION:[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What specific metric is being asked for?[0m                                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What time periods are involved?[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are there conversational references to resolve?[0m                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What type of calculation is needed (lookup, change, ratio, percentage)?[0m                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 2 - RESOLVE CONVERSATIONAL CONTEXT:[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- If question contains "that", "it", "this value" â†’ use the most recent result from conversation history[0m                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Example: Previous answer was 78.93, question asks "what is that divided by 100?" â†’ use 78.93[0m                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the previous year" â†’ identify specific year from context[0m                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the difference between the two values" â†’ use the two most recently mentioned values[0m                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 3 - DATA EXTRACTION:[0m                                                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Scan the ENTIRE table systematically (all rows, all columns)[0m                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Look for EXACT metric name matches first, then synonyms[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- When you see years (2012, 2014), distinguish:[0m                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Column headers (time periods) vs actual numeric values[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Don't confuse year labels with the data values[0m                                                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- For ambiguous cases, choose the value that makes business sense for the question[0m                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Percentage change: (new - old) / old[0m                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Differences: pay attention to order ("change from A to B" = B - A)[0m                                                                                                            [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Ratios: check question for correct numerator/denominator[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Preserve negative signs for declines, losses, decreases[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 5 - VERIFICATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Does the result magnitude make sense?[0m                                                                                                                                         [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are signs correct (positive/negative)?[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Is the scale appropriate?[0m                                                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mCOMMON ERROR PATTERNS TO AVOID:[0m                                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Don't return years (2012, 2014) when asked for financial values[0m                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Don't lose negative signs in calculations[0m                                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- For ambiguous cases, choose the value that makes business sense for the question[0m                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Preserve negative signs for declines, losses, decreases[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 1 - UNDERSTAND THE QUESTION:[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What specific metric is being asked for?[0m                                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What time periods are involved?[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are there conversational references to resolve?[0m                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What type of calculation is needed (lookup, change, ratio, percentage)?[0m                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 2 - RESOLVE CONVERSATIONAL CONTEXT:[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- If question contains "that", "it", "this value" â†’ use the most recent result from conversation history[0m                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Example: Previous answer was 78.93, question asks "what is that divided by 100?" â†’ use 78.93[0m                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the previous year" â†’ identify specific year from context[0m                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the difference between the two values" â†’ use the two most recently mentioned values[0m                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 3 - DATA EXTRACTION:[0m                                                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Scan the ENTIRE table systematically (all rows, all columns)[0m                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Look for EXACT metric name matches first, then synonyms[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- When you see years (2012, 2014), distinguish:[0m                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Column headers (time periods) vs actual numeric values[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Don't confuse year labels with the data values[0m                                                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- For ambiguous cases, choose the value that makes business sense for the question[0m                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Percentage change: (new - old) / old[0m                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Differences: pay attention to order ("change from A to B" = B - A)[0m                                                                                                            [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Ratios: check question for correct numerator/denominator[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Preserve negative signs for declines, losses, decreases[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 5 - VERIFICATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Does the result magnitude make sense?[0m                                                                                                                                         [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are signs correct (positive/negative)?[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Is the scale appropriate?[0m                                                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mCOMMON ERROR PATTERNS TO AVOID:[0m                                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mANALYSIS STRATEGY:[0m                                                                                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 1 - UNDERSTAND THE QUESTION:[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What specific metric is being asked for?[0m                                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What time periods are involved?[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are there conversational references to resolve?[0m                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What type of calculation is needed (lookup, change, ratio, percentage)?[0m                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 2 - RESOLVE CONVERSATIONAL CONTEXT:[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- If question contains "that", "it", "this value" â†’ use the most recent result from conversation history[0m                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Example: Previous answer was 78.93, question asks "what is that divided by 100?" â†’ use 78.93[0m                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the previous year" â†’ identify specific year from context[0m                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the difference between the two values" â†’ use the two most recently mentioned values[0m                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 3 - DATA EXTRACTION:[0m                                                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Scan the ENTIRE table systematically (all rows, all columns)[0m                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Look for EXACT metric name matches first, then synonyms[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- When you see years (2012, 2014), distinguish:[0m                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Column headers (time periods) vs actual numeric values[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Don't confuse year labels with the data values[0m                                                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- For ambiguous cases, choose the value that makes business sense for the question[0m                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Percentage change: (new - old) / old[0m                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Differences: pay attention to order ("change from A to B" = B - A)[0m                                                                                                            [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Ratios: check question for correct numerator/denominator[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Preserve negative signs for declines, losses, decreases[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 5 - VERIFICATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Does the result magnitude make sense?[0m                                                                                                                                         [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are signs correct (positive/negative)?[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Is the scale appropriate?[0m                                                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mCOMMON ERROR PATTERNS TO AVOID:[0m                                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mANALYSIS STRATEGY:[0m                                                                                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 1 - UNDERSTAND THE QUESTION:[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What specific metric is being asked for?[0m                                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What time periods are involved?[0m                                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are there conversational references to resolve?[0m                                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- What type of calculation is needed (lookup, change, ratio, percentage)?[0m                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 2 - RESOLVE CONVERSATIONAL CONTEXT:[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- If question contains "that", "it", "this value" â†’ use the most recent result from conversation history[0m                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Example: Previous answer was 78.93, question asks "what is that divided by 100?" â†’ use 78.93[0m                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the previous year" â†’ identify specific year from context[0m                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- "the difference between the two values" â†’ use the two most recently mentioned values[0m                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 3 - DATA EXTRACTION:[0m                                                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Scan the ENTIRE table systematically (all rows, all columns)[0m                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Look for EXACT metric name matches first, then synonyms[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- When you see years (2012, 2014), distinguish:[0m                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Column headers (time periods) vs actual numeric values[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m  * Don't confuse year labels with the data values[0m                                                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- For ambiguous cases, choose the value that makes business sense for the question[0m                                                                                              [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Percentage change: (new - old) / old[0m                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Differences: pay attention to order ("change from A to B" = B - A)[0m                                                                                                            [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Ratios: check question for correct numerator/denominator[0m                                                                                                                      [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Preserve negative signs for declines, losses, decreases[0m                                                                                                                       [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 5 - VERIFICATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                          [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Does the result magnitude make sense?[0m                                                                                                                                         [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Are signs correct (positive/negative)?[0m                                                                                                                                        [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Is the scale appropriate?[0m                                                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m                                                                                                                                                                                  [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mCOMMON ERROR PATTERNS TO AVOID:[0m                                                                                                                                                 [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Don't return years (2012, 2014) when asked for financial values[0m                                                                                                               [35mâ”‚[0m
[35mâ”‚[0m  [92m- Don't lose negative signs in calculations[0m                                                                                                                                     [35mâ”‚[0m

[35mâ”‚[0m  [92mSTEP 4 - CALCULATION:[0m                                                                                                                                                           [35mâ”‚[0m
